<Z>Christmas Games <C> I'm putting this out as super early warning. The games which are due to be run on Saturday 30th December <L.31.1>
(when I'll be away from New Year) will have a deadline of Thursday 28th December. I'm sure you'd rather have them turned around<L.31.1>
over the New Year break, and it means not having a rush to get the turn in with a short turnaround when we're back at work in<L.31.1>
in the New Year. So please make a note in your diaries etc now, that turn will have a deadline two days earlier than usual!<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Online Orders <C> If you aren't using the option for sending orders online (via www.softsim.co.uk) please let me know. It's<L.31.1>
much quicker, safer and more efficient than using snail mail, and significantly easier for me as well. <L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>9am Saturday <C> Please note that the deadline is 9am Saturday. It does seem since I've moved that Saturday morning is my<L.31.1>
optimum time for running games, so those who use post please don't send things Friday (delivery is about noon) and those who <L.31.1>
decide to wait until Saturday morning need to be early - there's a few of you who regularly miss the deadline, and in future I<L.31.1>
will simply crack on with games. Equally please don't chase me for "late" results until Monday - although I will generally aim to<L.31.1>
run Sunday, and I'm running the games in my spare time now, it's nice to have some flexibility over the weekend.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Other Games <C> If you aren't aware, I can generally sort out a second (or more) team in a game - I run more than one game of<L.31.1>
Gameplan Baseball, Hoopplan, Slapshot, Raceplan, Run Chase and Gameplan on a fortnightly basis (so I couldn't alternate games on<L.31.1>
different weeks) as well as Gridstats (NFL), Soccer Stats (Premier League) and Play On (AFL Aussie Rules) during their seasons on<L.31.1>
a weekly basis. If you fancy a new, or better, additional challenge, let me know and I can provide details.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Late Email Results <C> If you think results are late, please make sure you wait until the following morning before chasing up<L.31.1>
results. First step is to check out the Latest News at www.pbmsports.com - if I am running late I'll post a notice there (be aware<L.31.1>
you may need to refresh the page, in case you get an old copy from Cache memory). Please don't chase me up because you know your<L.31.1>
mate got his half an hour ago, because whilst most emails are "instant", often they do get delayed for a few hours and it does<L.31.1>
take a while to send them all out (I spread them out to avoid triggering firewalls).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>PDF Reports <C> Emailed game reports are available for all games here. The standard format is a PDF file - Adobe Reader is free<L.31.1>
to download (see www.pbmsports.com for a link) and you can open your reports with one click of the mouse and you can either view<L.31.1>
them on screen, or print them as you wish. You don't need to worry about formatting or printer drivers. The text format for<L.31.1>
reports is available but I only expect people will want to do so if they use the text file for other purposes (such as exporting<L.31.1>
the listings into software produced yourself). If you've not tried email reports before, try them out - it really is very easy. <L.31.1>
